# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements


Human cause almost 75% of all wildfires, 99.7%in Chile

Modeling approaches
 
> Physical: Simulate Fire Through  Mathematical Equations, high cost high accuracy

> Empirical: Use Historical Data, low cost low accuracy

> Coupled: Consider the interaction between fire and atmosphere Ex: FIRETEC, OpenFOAM

> Non-Coupled: Atmosphere-fire feedback is not explicitly included Ex: FARSITE, ELMFire, Phy-Fire  ^r0A9WZZ9

INTRO ^vXNTFhKn

> Physical:

> Empirical: ^oHdEuXrj

SIMPLIFIED COUPLED ATMOSPHERE-FIRE MODEL FOR SIMULATION OF 2D WILDLAND FIRES ^CzKED6k9

> Coupled:

> Non-Coupled: ^q6NNXUdF

MATHEMATICAL MODEL ^uXuvxJmc
